# BMCEngine
it's called bmcengine because it's made by bigmancozmo. get it? Get It? GET IT!?!?!!?!!?

##### *i think they get it*

###### *who knows*


# Compiling the engine
To compile the engine, you need one thing first.

[Visual Studio 2022](https://visualstudio.microsoft.com)

In the future you may need more things, like OpenGL/OpenAL/OpenCL. Open the .sln file with VS 2022. Then click the run button at the top. It's a green triangle with the word BMCEngine next to it.

now u have the engine
